I have taken my cars to The Garage for a few years now and my most recent experience was not a good one. I had taken my car in for a routine oil change and tire rotation. Prior to dropping off the car, I let them know that the Blind spot monitoring was malfunctioning and asked them to take a look at it. When I received the call that the car was ready for pickup, I was reassured that the technician had attempted on several occasions to test the blind spot monitoring and they found no issue with it. While on the phone I explained that the light on the dash was flashing and it had been happening since I last took it in when I got the battery replaced. Again, I was reassured that it was working cause he had just moved the car to the parking lot. When I arrived to pick up the car, it was noticed that the blind spot monitoring light was flashing on the dash and they had to then diagnose the issue and in the end I was informed that it's a software issue and they are unable to fix the problem.

< review>
The worst customer service I have ever worked with. I was a bartender for 15 years. Being in the industry I have worked with many companies. My friend ordered a jockey box, co2 tank and jockey box cover for his wedding. When I picked up the equipment I was told they gave away their last jockey box cover. Not sure why they would rent out a jockey box cover that they didnt have. I was also given a business card and was told by the owner that if I had any issues with the equipment to call the number and they would help me. Well, when we hooked up the jockey box and co2 tank with the supplied gasket, the co2 tank immediately leaked. I called the number on the card and left a message and never recieved a response. My friends beer ended up going flat within 2 hours of his wedding starting. It's obviously not good for the beer to go flat at a wedding. I returned the equipment and told them my issue. I was told the owner would get back to me. Well, that was almost a month ago. I have called probably 5 times. They finally answered when dialed *67 to not show my number. The owner answered and told me he was sorry and he would look into the issues and call me back. It has been 2 weeks since I talked to the owner and I have still not recieved a response. I have never dealt with  customer service this bad. I will be notifying the better business bureau.<//review>

< review>
Great experience using Beers in Sac. I rented a jockey box (two tap) to keep the beer cold for my wedding back in October. Worked like a charm. They were really flexible and allowed me to pick up the equipment on a Thursday for a Saturday event (no charge for the extra day) and return the equipment on the following Sunday afternoon. I mistakenly went to a "big wine/beer" store first and asked about renting a jockey box and everyone there said "oh no, you can't get those anywhere and if you can, they're super expensive and all that BS..." Naw. Go to Beers in Sac for all your beer dispensing needs. They're local, knowledgeable, friendly, priced well and they communicate well. I'll be going back to them the next time I throw a shindig. < Review>
Smog testing is a necessary evil, but we had a good experience here, I guess.

We'd been to two other smog test places that day, and believe-it-or-not, neither had anyone who could drive a stick shift!?

Who in their right mind would hire people for an auto-related business who can't drive a stick?

That wasn't a problem here, and we were in-and-out quickly.

Only reason I'm not giving five stars is because this place is pricier than most. Or, perhaps more accurately, we couldn't find any any website with coupons online for Compa Smog.<//Review>

Wow! Grocery pick up was so easy! Don't be daunted by the line to get in the store....

I hadn't done this during the initial throes of The After, but I did today. Amazon Prime via Whole Foods pick up at store service was great! I ordered about $130 worth of stuff, including wine(!) about an hour and a half before I wanted to pick it up and it was ready to go on time and correctly. They only had to make one substitution and I swear they threw the asparagus in for free. The shopper even brought it to my car for me. They have designated parking spots for pick up right outside the front door. I was a newbie and didn't see them, so he offered to bring them over. Sweet kid, tipping was very appreciated.

All in all, I was there maybe 5 min. Check in as soon as you arrive, or even a few minutes before if you're in a huge hurry. I just wasn't sure how the process worked at first, so I checked in after I parked, then realized I was supposed to park elsewhere and had to walk over to the front door to find him. Signage is really easy once you look up, LOL! 🤦🏻‍♀️
I truly hope this aspect remains a permanent part of life in The After. Looking forward to my next order!<//Review>
